    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText11853056736095571894" style="display:none">He thought he had it all. Everything was exactly how he wanted it to be. Until he found him.<br /><br />Brian Weber is almost like any other college student at the University of Wisconsin – Madison. He’s an English major hoping to become a journalist or a writer. Once his dorm roommate Andrew Engel moves in, his world changes completely. He’s the man he’s instantly hooked on. He admires everything about him from his athletic style to his varying interests. He’s drawn to be like him, overpowering everything else in his life. But there’s one surprise…<br /><br />Andrew is also gay.<br /><br />Their first date goes smoothly. Maybe a little too smoothly. Brian’s constantly worried he will say something awkward and ruin their relationship. Is it because he placed a sexual bet during a soccer match? Is it because he literally wants to be just like him? Maybe. Andrew’s quick to notice his desire to copy him, and he confronts him about it. Will their relationship last under this tight tension?</span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ❤︎ Riley ❤︎ by: </span>
      My sister

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3482856443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9107650707505689491"><b>4.5 Heart Filled Stars!</b><br/><br/><i> What kind of college dorm is this?</i><br/><br/>I tolerated my dorm roommate back when I was in college (please don't ask... you don't want to know), and this made me curious and picked the book up.<br/><br/>If I haven't gone to college... this book might make me want to go.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1583085035ra/29043078.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>This isn't what I expected when a friend of mine told me (or rather, me going through her book collection... <i>sorry sister!</i>) of this college roommate romance, I didn't think it was going to be like how it is. First off, I did</span>
  <span id="freeText9107650707505689491" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Heart Filled Stars!</b><br><br><i> What kind of college dorm is this?</i><br><br>I tolerated my dorm roommate back when I was in college (please don't ask... you don't want to know), and this made me curious and picked the book up.<br><br>If I haven't gone to college... this book might make me want to go.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1583085035ra/29043078.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This isn't what I expected when a friend of mine told me (or rather, me going through her book collection... <i>sorry sister!</i>) of this college roommate romance, I didn't think it was going to be like how it is. First off, I didn't expect Brian to literally copy his crush, Andrew. It's a desire he cannot stop even if he wanted to, and I'm glad Andrew accepted him for it. <br><br>However, there's one part that took me on a ride that I did not expect. The sex. I get college students are horny (yes, they are. don't deny it.), but I never thought someone would bang their roommate. Isn't that what frat houses are for?<br><br>But despite all of that, I quite enjoyed the story very much. I liked the theme of acceptance that Andrew provides for Brian. It's obvious from the beginning Brian is very insecure about himself, and is worried Andrew might leave him. Andrew's quick to respond with nothing but love and compassion for him, and that's what warmed my heart. Yes, the sex was hot and all, but it's that love and acceptance that got me hooked on it.<br><br>I pre-ordered the sequel, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/54244818.The_Change_in_the_Heart__Change__2_" title="The Change in the Heart (Change #2) by B.Q. Hanson" rel="nofollow noopener">The Change in the Heart</a> and I cannot wait to read it!<br><br></span>

<div id="review_3378190980" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="***Ivy***" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/116493385-ivy"><img alt="***Ivy***" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591486853p2/116493385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3378190980?book_show_action=true">Jun 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="***Ivy***" class="user" itemprop="url" name="***Ivy***" href="/user/show/116493385-ivy">***Ivy***</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/116493385-ivy?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/116493385-ivy?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3378190980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7639321525616374417">Thank you so much for the arc copy!<br/><br/>Here's my breakdown:<br/>Cover: 4/5<br/>Story: 4.5/5<br/>Characters: 4.5/5<br/>Tension (oh boy there was a lot of it!) 5/5<br/>Total: 4.5ish/5<br/><br/>When I first read this, I was deeply intrigued buy the thought process and experience of the MC Brian. At first, I was going to think this was a rewrite of the book and film Single White Female, but to my avail it was much better than that. Brian Weber is dealing with a massive amount of struggles, mainly with self worth, self image, and so on. H</span>
  <span id="freeText7639321525616374417" style="display:none">Thank you so much for the arc copy!<br /><br />Here's my breakdown:<br />Cover: 4/5<br />Story: 4.5/5<br />Characters: 4.5/5<br />Tension (oh boy there was a lot of it!) 5/5<br />Total: 4.5ish/5<br /><br />When I first read this, I was deeply intrigued buy the thought process and experience of the MC Brian. At first, I was going to think this was a rewrite of the book and film Single White Female, but to my avail it was much better than that. Brian Weber is dealing with a massive amount of struggles, mainly with self worth, self image, and so on. His romantic journey starts when he starts school at university and meets his dorm mate Andrew. From there, it's very much love at first sight. He's deeply interested in Andrew's hobbies and personality. This causes him to find that Andrew is the person who he's meant to be like, but never knew it ever before. This whole story revolves around the notion of Brian wanting to be like Andrew all while Andrew wants him to be who he truly is.<br /><br />I truly enjoyed this story and it's characters. I actually felt a slight connection with Brian and his struggles and that's something that I just cannot say for many of the books I've read. I enjoyed the tight tension as it always made me want to know what's coming up. <br /><br />I would highly recommend this book for an interesting read.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7639321525616374417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3351132293" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3351132293" />
    <a title="Joyce" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/114718779-joyce"><img alt="Joyce" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588784798p2/114718779.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3351132293?book_show_action=true">May 25, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Joyce" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Joyce" href="/user/show/114718779-joyce">Joyce</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=beta-read">beta-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=college">college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/114718779-joyce?shelf=quirky">quirky</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3351132293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8125249968700635502">*** Beta Read ***<br/><br/>This story is very quirky, in fact, it's one of the most unique love stories I've read in a while. The story follows the college adventures of Brian Weber and his roommate Andrew Engel. Brain moves into the dorms and is immediately struck by his roommate. It was love at first sight for Brain, but not so much for Andrew. *This is where the quirkiness comes in* One of the biggest desires Brian has for Andrew is to be like his image. Upon finding out the things he likes, he quickly</span>
  <span id="freeText8125249968700635502" style="display:none">*** Beta Read ***<br /><br />This story is very quirky, in fact, it's one of the most unique love stories I've read in a while. The story follows the college adventures of Brian Weber and his roommate Andrew Engel. Brain moves into the dorms and is immediately struck by his roommate. It was love at first sight for Brain, but not so much for Andrew. *This is where the quirkiness comes in* One of the biggest desires Brian has for Andrew is to be like his image. Upon finding out the things he likes, he quickly falls in love with those characteristics and claims them as his own, becoming a fan of various sports when he never originally liked such things. Andrew's quick to notice this, and he's there to support him. Brian's biggest fear is him running away from him, but he's willing to make Brian more comfortable with himself and to make sure he's accepted with him.<br /><br />Now for my review; I really enjoyed this story. The idea of loving someone and who they are so much to the point where you want to be like them is definitely quirky. This trope isn't touched on much (if at all) in romance and I'm certainly glad the author incorporated it. One aspect I enjoyed the most if the fact that Brian loves Andrew for who he is and exactly who he is, and he makes this point clear, and that he doesn't want him to change to try and impress him. Now THAT is something I love seeing, especially considering our society tends to push people into being who they aren't just to fit in, and this combats that.<br /><br />Overall, I recommend this story if you want to read a quirky story. <br /><br />ps: I cannot wait for the sequel and this one isn't even out yet</span>
  <a data-text-id="8125249968700635502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3581886244" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3581886244" />
    <a title="✯Reading to the Stars!✯" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/122481082-reading-to-the-stars"><img alt="✯Reading to the Stars!✯" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601925566p2/122481082.jpg" /></a>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AZcW8HMGRgyrVHi/0ejYfKNTiO+YCAKmjHKtQhS6UK87sX8iyFiPZAx/zN4mHdKjdQxvJ1aFjMHXDOvz2fmiNQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JHw3xdwAnwpPQp5TxqHFPMBwNOKowrkPEI7DRYHthEAeWl4XZ15WYuhpKjIxVM/jFi/TKmZPN2hL8IX0TK522g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Over the course of his career, the chef struggled with suicidal thoughts, depression and anxiety. He shied away from praise and begged not to be given awards.
